function blink_g1() {
    TweenLite.to(eye_1, .3, {
            autoAlpha:0, delay:Math.floor(4*Math.random())+1, ease:g_lights, onComplete:function() {
                TweenLite.to(eye_1, .3, {
                        autoAlpha:1, ease:g_lights, onComplete:blink_g1
                    }

                )
            }
        }

    )
}

            autoAlpha:0, delay:Math.floor(3*Math.random())+1, ease:g_lights, onComplete:function() {
                TweenLite.to(eye_2, .3, {
                        autoAlpha:1, ease:g_lights, onComplete:blink_g2
                    }

                )
            }
        }

    )
}
